MDO BCU DANG RGYUD BLA MA DANG DUS 'KHOR

NYID, ,DE NYID DU NA DE MA SKYES, ,MA SKYES PA NI MA 'GAG NYID,
CES DANG, NGO BO NYID KYIS SKYES PAR NI, ,DON DAM DU NI DE BKAG
PHYIR, ZHES DANG, DBU MA SNYING PO LAS

DE'I PHYIR CHOS THAMS CAD MI RTAG PA LA SOGS PA JI LTAR RNAM PAR
BZHAG PA'I MTSAN NYID DON DAM PAS STONG PA'I PHYIR, MA SKYES PA
YIN NO, ,DE'I PHYIR MA 'GAG PA YIN NO, ,DE'I PHYIR GZOD MA NAS
ZHI BA YIN NO, ,DE'I PHYIR

RANG BZHIN GYIS YONGS SU MYA NGAN LAS 'DAS PA YIN NO, ZHES DANG,
DGONGS 'GREL LAS, GANG RANG GI MTSAN NYID KYIS MED PA DE NI MA
SKYES PA'O GANG MA SKYES PA DE NI MA 'GAG PA'O, ,GANG MA 'GAG PA
DE NI GZOD MA NAS ZHI

PA'O, ,ZHES SOGS DRANGS SO, ZHI 'TSO SOGS KYIS SEMS TZAM PA'I
MTSAN NYID GSUM DGONGS 'GREL SOGS KYIS BSTAN DON PHAL BA DANG
RANG LUGS KYI MTSAN NYID GSUM DNGOS BSTAN DU BZHED KYANG LEGS
LDAN GYIS DE DAG

GI DON DU MI BZHED DO, ,GNYIS PA RANG LUGS MTSAN NYID GSUM NI,
STONG GZHI BDEN PA RTAGS CHA DANG DES STONG BA, ,RIM BZHIN GZHAN
DBANG KUN BTAGS YONGS GRUB STE, ,RANG DBANG MIN PHYIR BRTAGS
PHYIR GNAS LUGS PHYIR, ZHES SMRA

@110A *, ,TE; TSIG RKANG GSUM GYIS CHOS CAN DANG CHOS DANG RTAGS
RNAMS RIM BZHIN SBYAR NAS BSHAD RIGS TE, GANG ZHIG GANG DANG
'BREL BA NI, ,RING NA 'DUG KYANG DE DANG DE, ZHES GRAGS PA'I
PHYIR RO, ,STONG GZHI

GZUGS SOGS KYI DNGOS PO CHOS CAN, GZHAN DBANG DANG SKYE BA NGO BO
NYID MED PA ZHES BYA STE, KHYOD RKYEN GZHAN LA LTOS NAS SKYE BAS
NA DON DAM PA RANG BZHIN NAM, DON DAM PAR RANG DBANG GIS SKYE BA
MED PAS DE LTAR

BRJOD PA'I PHYIR TE, MA DROS PAS ZHUS PA LAS GANG ZHIG RKYEN LAS
SKYES PA DE MA SKYES, ,DE LA SKYE BA'I RANG BZHIN YOD MA YIN,
,RKYEN LA RAG LAS GANG DE STONG BAR BSHAD, ,GANG ZHIG STONG NYID
SHES DE BAG YOD YIN, ZHES DANG

DAG NGO BO NYID KYIS MED, SOGS MDO DU MA DANG, 'PHAGS PA'I ZHABS
KYIS, RANG BZHIN RGYU DANG RKYEN DAG LAS, ,'BYUNG BAR RIGS PA MA
YIN TE, SOGS DANG,

DBU MA SNANG BA LAS, DE LA DNGOS PO MA BRTAGS NA, ZHES PA NAS, DE
YANG KUN RDZOB TU SGYU MA BZHIN DU GZHAN GYI RKYEN GYI DBANG GIS
SKYE YI BDAG NYID KHO NA NI MA YIN PAS, SKYE BA NGO BO NYID MED
PA NYID DU RNAM PAR BZHAG STE,
